c25c8c232337fe57c1bd117210979dd5cc8f7178 ACCUMULO-19 - provides three packages, and the templates for some more for the future. Accumulo is the bare bones install, accumulo-native will introduce the code neccessary to build the native libraries and build them, and accumulo-test imports all of the testing code under ACCUMULO_HOME/test. There are control files for future files, but they are not developed, but I think they are fairly straightforward. Everything installs to /usr/lib/accumulo, with symlinks for the conf directory pointing to /etc/accumulo/conf (with all example files copied into that directory). Additional symlinks are made from logs and walogs to /var/log/accumulo/log and walog respectively. Remove leaves everything in /var/log/accumulo and /etc/accumulo/ intact. Purge will remove them. Accumulo-native is tied directly to the accumulo version. I have nothing in place with regard to upgrades and things like that, but I don't think that is necessary, at least for now.
